***поцелуй.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелу́й</a> (3460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pocelovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the present stem (compare first singular <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелу́ю</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pocelúju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцеловать.html>поцелу́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pocelúj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцелуй.html>поцелу́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцелуй.html>поцелу́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поцелуй.html>поцелу́ев</a></b>)
</p>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="региональное">рег.</span> что-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:начатый.html>на́чатое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:початый.html>початое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цельный.html>це́льное</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отнятый.html>отнята</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отделённый.html>отделена́</a> какая-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:початок.html>Поча́ток</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:пирога.html>пирога</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почать.html>поча́ть</a> (20654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почать.html>поча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">почина́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to consume</li></ol>

***почва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a> (3075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">подъшьва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podŭšĭva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sole (bottom); foundation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́шва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podóšva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sole, (mountain) foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póčva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чвы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чвы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>earth, soil, ground (mixture of sand and organic material)</li>
<li>basis, base, ground</li></ol>

***почему.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> (119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">according to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чему́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čemú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počemú</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative adverb</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> why? <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">on what ground; according to what</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Počemú</b> vy govoríte éto?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why do you say this?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Počemú</b> on želájet vídetʹ menjá?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why does he wish to see me?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>For the answer, directly coordinate only with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as well as with the solitary responses <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтому.html>поэ́тому</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poétomu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The literary <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ибо.html>и́бо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">íbo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> also fulfills a close role to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">potomú što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почерпнуть.html>почерпну́ть</a> (17052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">черпну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čerpnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почерпнуть.html>почерпну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počerpnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to get, to draw, to derive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:почерпнуть.html>почерпну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сведение.html>сведения</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>počerpnútʹ</b> svedenija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pick up information</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:почерпнуть.html>почерпну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>počerpnútʹ</b> znánija iz knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive knowledge from books</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***почесать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почесать.html>почеса́ть</a> (6537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чесать.html>чеса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">česátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почесать.html>почеса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počesátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чесать.html>чеса́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to comb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">textiles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to card, to comb</li>
<li>to scratch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почесать.html>почеса́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">počesátʹ jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wag one's tongue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почесать.html>почеса́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затылок.html>заты́лок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">počesátʹ zatýlok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scratch one's head</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Analyzable as deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почесть.html>поче́сть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">počéstʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare past adverbial participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почесть.html>почётши</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">počótši</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почечный.html>по́чечный</a> (13565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почка.html>по́чка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póčka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почечный.html>по́чечный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póčečnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>renal</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">аорта́льно-по́чечный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aortálʹno-póčečnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">činítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***почистить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:почистить.html>почи́стить</a> (10222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почистить.html>почи́стить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">počístitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clean, to scour</li>
<li>to peel</li></ol>
